❯ The following request was developed in conjunction with "regualar" Claude: Task: Generate 50 simple Q&A pairs
for SFT training, drawn from vocabulary found in this corpus file:
txt_local/corpus_of_gutenberg_novels_cleaned_shuffled_2026_03_03_B.txt
(or equivalently from one or more of the smaller ‘fragment’ files).

Method: Sample random passages from the corpus. From each passage, pick individual words — nouns, verbs,

adjectives — that are interesting or slightly uncommon. Generate a short question and a short answer about each

word.

Question types to vary across:

* "What does [word] mean?"

* "What is a [noun]?"

* "What color/shape/size is a [noun]?"

* "What does it mean to [verb]?"

* "Describe a [noun]."

* "What is the opposite of [adjective]?"

Rules:

* All text lowercase, no numbers

* Questions under 10 words

* Answers under 15 words

* One Q&A pair per line in JSONL format: {"question": "...", "answer": "..."}

* No duplicate words

* Draw vocabulary only from words actually found in the corpus

* Output to sft_data/round1_vocab.jsonl

Examples:

1. Q: What does plundered mean? A: stripped of everything valuable.

2. Q: What is a captive? A: a person who is held against their will.

3. Q: What color are flames? A: flames are red and gold.

4. Q: What is a highland brigade? A: a group of soldiers from the highlands.

5. Q: What does withered mean? A: dry and shrunken, usually from age.

mean? A: stripped of everything valuable.
2. Q: What is a captive? A: a person who is held against their will.
3. Q: What color are flames? A: flames are red and gold.
4. Q: What is a highland brigade? A: a group of soldiers from the highlands.

5. Q: What does withered mean? A: dry and shrunken, usually from age.

6. Q: Who is a sovereign? A: a king or queen who rules a country.

7. Q: Where was a garrison kept? A: in a fort or walled town.

8. Q: Why did he retreat? A: to escape danger or a stronger enemy.

9. Q: Who is a governess? A: a woman hired to teach children at home.

10. Q: Where was the hearth? A: in front of the fireplace.

11. Q: Why did she weep? A: because of grief or sorrow.

12. Q: Who is an adjutant? A: an officer who assists a commander.

13. Q: Where was the rampart? A: along the outer wall of a fortress.

14. Q: Why did they flee? A: to escape from approaching danger.

15. Q: Who is a valet? A: a personal servant to a gentleman.

❯ The following request was developed in conjunction with "regualar" Claude: Task: Generate 50 simple Q&A pairs

for SFT training, drawn from vocabulary found in this corpus file:

txt_local/corpus_of_gutenberg_novels_cleaned_shuffled_2026_03_03_B.txt

(or equivalently from one or more of the smaller ‘fragment’ files).

Method: Sample random passages from the corpus. From each passage, pick individual words — nouns, verbs,

adjectives — that are interesting or slightly uncommon. Generate a short question and a short answer about each

word.

Question types to vary across:

* "What does [word] mean?"

* "What is a [noun]?"

* "What color/shape/size is a [noun]?"

* "What does it mean to [verb]?"

* "Describe a [noun]."

* "What is the opposite of [adjective]?"

Rules:

* All text lowercase, no numbers

* Questions under 10 words

* Answers under 15 words

* One Q&A pair per line in JSONL format: {"question": "...", "answer": "..."}

* No duplicate words

* Draw vocabulary only from words actually found in the corpus

* Output to sft_data/round1_vocab.jsonl

Examples:

1. Q: What does plundered mean? A: stripped of everything valuable.

2. Q: What is a captive? A: a person who is held against their will.

3. Q: What color are flames? A: flames are red and gold.

4. Q: What is a highland brigade? A: a group of soldiers from the highlands.

5. Q: What does withered mean? A: dry and shrunken, usually from age.
